Hi Manuel,

Please see the attached invoice to extend the pilot for another quarter -
Q1 2016 (January 1 - March 31, 2016).

The pilot extension is for the same terms as outlined our original Sep 22,
2015 Proposal (attached). Key pricing and payment terms are:
- 3 months at $750/month = $2,250 will be billed to your card on file
- Up to 500 employees
- Payment terms Net 15. No refunds.

The purpose of the pilot extension is to continue giving access to "ninjas"
(key internal community managers), with the goal of getting more knowledge
archived and indexed inside of Luno, and then opening access up to the rest
of TSF and TSL before the end of the quarter.

If this all looks ok to you, can you expressly give permission to charge
your card on file for the pilot extension by replying with:

"I grant Luno permission to charge the Visa ending in -5082 for the
TT.Jan.2016 Invoice for the full amount of $2,250 to extend the Luno pilot
through Q1 2016."


Thanks!
allen
